<s> At its outset it had been terrible </s>
<s> It had engulfed Hicks's army, swept over Gordon and Khartoum, rolled behind the British forces as they retired down the river, and finally cast up a spray of raiding parties as far north as Assouan </s>
<s> Then it found other channels to east and to west, to Central Africa and to Abyssinia, and retired a little on the side of Egypt </s>
<s> For ten years there ensued a lull, during which the frontier garrisons looked out upon those distant blue hills of Dongola </s>
<s> Behind the violet mists which draped them, lay a land of blood and horror </s>
<s> From time to time some adventurer went south towards those haze-girt mountains, tempted by stories of gum and ivory, but none ever returned </s>
<s> Once a mutilated Egyptian and once a Greek woman, mad with thirst and fear, made their way to the lines </s>
<s> They were the only exports of that country of darkness </s>
<s> Sometimes the sunset would turn those distant mists into a bank of crimson, and the dark mountains would rise from that sinister reek like islands in a sea of blood </s>
<s> It seemed a grim symbol in the southern heaven when seen from the fort-capped hills by Wady Halfa </s>
<s> Ten years of lust in Khartoum, ten years of silent work in Cairo, and then all was ready, and it was time for civilisation to take a trip south once more, travelling, as her wont is, in an armoured train </s>
<s> Everything was ready, down to the last pack-saddle of the last camel, and yet no one suspected it, for an unconstitutional Government has its advantages </s>
<s> A great administrator had argued, and managed, and cajoled; a great soldier had organised and planned, and made piastres do the work of pounds </s>
<s> And then one night these two master spirits met and clasped hands, and the soldier vanished away upon some business of his own </s>
<s> And just at that very time Bimbashi Hilary Joyce, seconded from the Royal Mallow Fusiliers, and temporarily attached to the Ninth Soudanese, made his first appearance in Cairo </s>
<s> Napoleon had said, and Hilary Joyce had noted, that great reputations are only to be made in the East </s>
<s> Here he was in the East with four tin cases of baggage, a Wilkinson sword, a Bond's slug-throwing pistol, and a copy of _Green's Introduction to the Study of Arabic_ </s>
<s> With such a start, and the blood of youth running hot in his veins, everything seemed easy </s>
<s> He was a little frightened of the General, he had heard stories of his sternness to young officers, but with tact and suavity he hoped for the best </s>
<s> So, leaving his effects at Shepheard's Hotel, he reported himself at headquarters </s>
<s> It was not the General, but the head of the Intelligence Department who received him, the Chief being still absent upon that business which had called him </s>
<s> Hilary Joyce found himself in the presence of a short, thick-set officer, with a gentle voice and a placid expression which covered a remarkably acute and energetic spirit </s>
<s> With that quiet smile and guileless manner he had undercut and outwitted the most cunning of Orientals </s>
<s> He stood, a cigarette between his fingers, looking at the new-comer </s>
<s> "I heard that you had come </s>
<s> Sorry the Chief isn't here to see you </s>
<s> Gone up to the frontier, you know" </s>
<s> "My regiment is at Wady Halfa </s>
<s> I suppose, sir, that I should report myself there at once" </s>
<s> "No; I was to give you your orders" </s>
<s> He led the way to a map upon the wall, and pointed with the end of his cigarette </s>
<s> "You see this place </s>
<s> It's the Oasis of Kurkur--a little quiet, I am afraid, but excellent air </s>
<s> You are to get out there as quick as possible </s>
<s> You'll find a company of the Ninth, and half a squadron of cavalry </s>
<s> You will be in command" </s>
<s> Hilary Joyce looked at the name, printed at the intersection of two black lines, without another dot upon the map for several inches round it </s>
<s> "A village, sir" </s>
<s> "No, a well </s>
<s> Not very good water, I'm afraid, but you soon get accustomed to natron </s>
<s> It's an important post, as being at the junction of two caravan routes </s>
<s> All routes are closed now, of course, but still you never know who _might_ come along them" </s>
<s> "We are there, I presume, to prevent raiding" </s>
<s> "Well, between you and me, there's really nothing to raid </s>
<s> You are there to intercept messengers </s>
<s> They must call at the wells </s>

<s> Railway to Baliani, the post-boat to Assouan, and then two days on a camel in the Libyan Desert, with an Ababdeh guide, and three baggage-camels to tie one down to their own exasperating pace </s>
<s> However, even two and a half miles an hour mount up in time, and at last, on the third evening, from the blackened slag-heap of a hill which is called the Jebel Kurkur, Hilary Joyce looked down upon a distant clump of palms, and thought that this cool patch of green in the midst of the merciless blacks and yellows was the fairest colour effect that he had ever seen </s>
<s> An hour later he had ridden into the little camp, the guard had turned out to salute him, his native subordinate had greeted him in excellent English, and he had fairly entered into his own </s>
<s> It was not an exhilarating place for a lengthy residence </s>
<s> There was one large bowl-shaped, grassy depression sloping down to the three pits of brown and brackish water </s>
<s> There was the grove of palm trees also, beautiful to look upon, but exasperating in view of the fact that Nature has provided her least shady trees on the very spot where shade is needed most </s>
<s> A single widespread acacia did something to restore the balance </s>
<s> Here Hilary Joyce slumbered in the heat, and in the cool he inspected his square-shouldered, spindle-shanked Soudanese, with their cheery black faces and their funny little pork-pie forage caps </s>
<s> Joyce was a martinet at drill, and the blacks loved being drilled, so the Bimbashi was soon popular among them </s>
<s> But one day was exactly like another </s>
<s> The weather, the view, the employment, the food--everything was the same </s>
<s> At the end of three weeks he felt that he had been there for interminable years </s>
<s> And then at last there came something to break the monotony </s>
<s> One evening, as the sun was sinking, Hilary Joyce rode slowly down the old caravan road </s>
<s> It had a fascination for him, this narrow track, winding among the boulders and curving up the nullahs, for he remembered how in the map it had gone on and on, stretching away into the unknown heart of Africa </s>
<s> The countless pads of innumerable camels through many centuries had beaten it smooth, so that now, unused and deserted, it still wound away, the strangest of roads, a foot broad, and perhaps two thousand miles in length </s>
<s> Joyce wondered as he rode how long it was since any traveller had journeyed up it from the south, and then he raised his eyes, and there was a man coming along the path </s>
<s> For an instant Joyce thought that it might be one of his own men, but a second glance assured him that this could not be so </s>
<s> The stranger was dressed in the flowing robes of an Arab, and not in the close-fitting khaki of a soldier </s>
<s> He was very tall, and a high turban made him seem gigantic </s>
<s> He strode swiftly along, with head erect, and the bearing of a man who knows no fear </s>
<s> Who could he be, this formidable giant coming out of the unknown </s>
<s> The percursor possibly of a horde of savage spearmen </s>
<s> And where could he have walked from </s>
<s> The nearest well was a long hundred miles down the track </s>
<s> At any rate the frontier post of Kurkur could not afford to receive casual visitors </s>
<s> Hilary Joyce whisked round his horse, galloped into camp, and gave the alarm </s>
<s> Then, with twenty horsemen at his back, he rode out again to reconnoitre </s>
<s> The man was still coming on in spite of these hostile preparations </s>
<s> For an instant he had hesitated when first he saw the cavalry, but escape was out of the question, and he advanced with the air of one who makes the best of a bad job </s>
<s> He made no resistance, and said nothing when the hands of two troopers clutched at his shoulders, but walked quietly between their horses into camp </s>

<s> There were no signs of any Dervishes </s>

<s> II THE SURGEON OF GASTER FELL I: HOW THE WOMAN CAME TO KIRKBY-MALHOUSE Bleak and wind-swept is the little town of Kirkby-Malhouse, harsh and forbidding are the fells upon which it stands </s>
<s> It stretches in a single line of grey-stone, slate-roofed houses, dotted down the furze-clad slope of the rolling moor </s>
<s> In this lonely and secluded village, I, James Upperton, found myself in the summer of '85 </s>
<s> Little as the hamlet had to offer, it contained that for which I yearned above all things--seclusion and freedom from all which might distract my mind from the high and weighty subjects which engaged it </s>
<s> But the inquisitiveness of my landlady made my lodgings undesirable and I determined to seek new quarters </s>
<s> As it chanced, I had in one of my rambles come upon an isolated dwelling in the very heart of these lonely moors, which I at once determined should be my own </s>
<s> It was a two-roomed cottage, which had once belonged to some shepherd, but had long been deserted, and was crumbling rapidly to ruin </s>
<s> In the winter floods, the Gaster Beck, which runs down Gaster Fell, where the little dwelling stood, had overswept its banks and torn away a part of the wall </s>
<s> The roof was in ill case, and the scattered slates lay thick amongst the grass </s>
<s> Yet the main shell of the house stood firm and true; and it was no great task for me to have all that was amiss set right </s>
<s> The two rooms I laid out in a widely different manner--my own tastes are of a Spartan turn, and the outer chamber was so planned as to accord with them </s>
<s> An oil-stove by Rippingille of Birmingham furnished me with the means of cooking; while two great bags, the one of flour, and the other of potatoes, made me independent of all supplies from without </s>
<s> In diet I had long been a Pythagorean, so that the scraggy, long-limbed sheep which browsed upon the wiry grass by the Gaster Beck had little to fear from their new companion </s>
<s> A nine-gallon cask of oil served me as a sideboard; while a square table, a deal chair and a truckle-bed completed the list of my domestic fittings </s>
<s> At the head of my couch hung two unpainted shelves--the lower for my dishes and cooking utensils, the upper for the few portraits which took me back to the little that was pleasant in the long, wearisome toiling for wealth and for pleasure which had marked the life I had left behind </s>
<s> If this dwelling-room of mine were plain even to squalor, its poverty was more than atoned for by the luxury of the chamber which was destined to serve me as my study </s>
<s> I had ever held that it was best for my mind to be surrounded by such objects as would be in harmony with the studies which occupied it, and that the loftiest and most ethereal conditions of thought are only possible amid surroundings which please the eye and gratify the senses </s>
<s> The room which I had set apart for my mystic studies was set forth in a style as gloomy and majestic as the thoughts and aspirations with which it was to harmonise </s>
<s> Both walls and ceilings were covered with a paper of the richest and glossiest black, on which was traced a lurid and arabesque pattern of dead gold </s>
<s> A black velvet curtain covered the single diamond-paned window; while a thick, yielding carpet of the same material prevented the sound of my own footfalls, as I paced backward and forward, from breaking the current of my thought </s>
<s> Along the cornices ran gold rods, from which depended six pictures, all of the sombre and imaginative caste, which chimed best with my fancy </s>
<s> And yet it was destined that ere ever I reached this quiet harbour I should learn that I was still one of humankind, and that it is an ill thing to strive to break the bond which binds us to our fellows </s>
<s> It was but two nights before the date I had fixed upon for my change of dwelling, when I was conscious of a bustle in the house beneath, with the bearing of heavy burdens up the creaking stair, and the harsh voice of my landlady, loud in welcome and protestations of joy </s>
<s> From time to time, amid the whirl of words, I could hear a gentle and softly modulated voice, which struck pleasantly upon my ear after the long weeks during which I had listened only to the rude dialect of the dalesmen </s>
<s> For an hour I could hear the dialogue beneath--the high voice and the low, with clatter of cup and clink of spoon, until at last a light, quick step passed my study door, and I knew that my new fellow-lodger had sought her room </s>
<s> On the morning after this incident I was up be-times, as is my wont; but I was surprised, on glancing from my window, to see that our new inmate was earlier still </s>
<s> She was walking down the narrow pathway, which zigzags over the fell--a tall woman, slender, her head sunk upon her breast, her arms filled with a bristle of wild flowers, which she had gathered in her morning rambles </s>
<s> The white and pink of her dress, and the touch of deep red ribbon in her broad drooping hat, formed a pleasant dash of colour against the dun-tinted landscape </s>
<s> She was some distance off when I first set eyes upon her, yet I knew that this wandering woman could be none other than our arrival of last night, for there was a grace and refinement in her bearing which marked her from the dwellers of the fells </s>
<s> Even as I watched she passed swiftly and lightly down the pathway, and turning through the wicket gate, at the further end of our cottage garden, she seated herself upon the green bank which faced my window, and strewing her flowers in front of her, set herself to arrange them </s>
<s> As she sat there, with the rising sun at her back, and the glow of the morning spreading like an aureole around her stately and well-poised head, I could see that she was a woman of extraordinary personal beauty </s>
<s> Her face was Spanish rather than English in its type--oval, olive, with black, sparkling eyes, and a sweetly sensitive mouth </s>
<s> From under the broad straw hat two thick coils of blue-black hair curved down on either side of her graceful queenly neck </s>
<s> I was surprised, as I watched her, to see that her shoes and skirt bore witness to a journey rather than to a mere morning ramble </s>
<s> Her light dress was stained, wet and bedraggled; while her boots were thick with the yellow soil of the fells </s>
<s> Her face, too, wore a weary expression, and her young beauty seemed to be clouded over by the shadow of inward trouble </s>
<s> Even as I watched her, she burst suddenly into wild weeping, and throwing down her bundle of flowers ran swiftly into the house </s>
<s> Distrait as I was and weary of the ways of the world, I was conscious of a sudden pang of sympathy and grief as I looked upon the spasm of despair which seemed to convulse this strange and beautiful woman </s>
<s> I bent to my books, and yet my thoughts would ever turn to her proud clear-cut face, her weather-stained dress, her drooping head, and the sorrow which lay in each line and feature of her pensive face </s>

<s> Even my study had not been safe from this rough intruder, for the prints of a heavy boot were plainly visible on the ebony-black carpet </s>
<s> IV: OF THE MAN WHO CAME IN THE NIGHT The night set in gusty and tempestuous, and the moon was all girt with ragged clouds </s>
<s> The wind blew in melancholy gusts, sobbing and sighing over the moor, and setting all the gorse bushes agroaning </s>
<s> From time to time a little sputter of rain pattered up against the window-pane </s>
<s> I sat until near midnight, glancing over the fragment on immortality by Iamblichus, the Alexandrian platonist, of whom the Emperor Julian said that he was posterior to Plato in time but not in genius </s>
<s> At last, shutting up my book, I opened my door and took a last look at the dreary fell and still more dreary sky </s>
<s> As I protruded my head, a swoop of wind caught me and sent the red ashes of my pipe sparkling and dancing through the darkness </s>
<s> At the same moment the moon shone brilliantly out from between two clouds and I saw, sitting on the hillside, not two hundred yards from my door, the man who called himself the surgeon of Gaster Fell </s>
<s> He was squatted among the heather, his elbows upon his knees, and his chin resting upon his hands, as motionless as a stone, with his gaze fixed steadily upon the door of my dwelling </s>
<s> At the sight of this ill-omened sentinel, a chill of horror and of fear shot through me, for his gloomy and mysterious associations had cast a glamour round the man, and the hour and place were in keeping with his sinister presence </s>

<s> he cried </s>

<s> For two days the wind freshened and increased, with constant squalls of rain until on the third night the most furious storm was raging which I can ever recollect in England </s>
<s> I felt that it was positively useless to go to bed, nor could I concentrate my mind sufficiently to read a book </s>
<s> I turned my lamp half down to moderate the glare, and leaning back in my chair, I gave myself up to reverie </s>

<s> And what was the meaning of it all </s>
<s> you ask </s>
<s> Many a drama which I have come across in my wandering life, some as strange and as striking as this one, has lacked the ultimate explanation which you demand </s>

<s> "KIRKBY LUNATIC ASYLUM, "_September 4th_, 1885 </s>
<s> "SIR,--I am deeply conscious that some apology and explanation is due to you for the very startling and, in your eyes, mysterious events which have recently occurred, and which have so seriously interfered with the retired existence which you desire to lead </s>
<s> I should have called upon you on the morning after the recapture of my father, but my knowledge of your dislike to visitors and also of--you will excuse my saying it--your very violent temper, led me to think that it was better to communicate with you by letter </s>
<s> "My poor father was a hard-working general practitioner in Birmingham, where his name is still remembered and respected </s>
<s> About ten years ago he began to show signs of mental aberration, which we were inclined to put down to overwork and the effects of a sunstroke </s>
<s> Feeling my own incompetence to pronounce upon a case of such importance, I at once sought the highest advice in Birmingham and London </s>
<s> Among others we consulted the eminent alienist, Mr Fraser Brown, who pronounced my father's case to be intermittent in its nature, but dangerous during the paroxysms </s>
<s> 'It may take a homicidal, or it may take a religious turn,' he said; 'or it may prove to be a mixture of both </s>
<s> For months he may be as well as you or I, and then in a moment he may break out </s>
<s> You will incur a great responsibility if you leave him without supervision' </s>
<s> "I need say no more, sir </s>
<s> You will understand the terrible task which has fallen upon my poor sister and me in endeavoring to save my father from the asylum which in his sane moments filled him with horror </s>
<s> I can only regret that your peace has been disturbed by our misfortunes, and I offer you in my sister's name and my own our apologies </s>
<s> "Yours truly, "J </s>

<s> III BORROWED SCENES "It cannot be done </s>
<s> People really would not stand it </s>
<s> I know because I have tried".--_Extract from an unpublished paper upon George Borrow and his writings._ Yes, I tried and my experience may interest other people </s>
<s> You must imagine, then, that I am soaked in George Borrow, especially in his _Lavengro_ and his _Romany Rye_, that I have modelled both my thoughts, my speech and my style very carefully upon those of the master, and that finally I set forth one summer day actually to lead the life of which I had read </s>

<s> IV THE MAN FROM ARCHANGEL On the fourth day of March, in the year 1867, I being at that time in my five-and-twentieth year, I wrote down the following words in my note-book--the result of much mental perturbation and conflict: "The solar system, amidst a countless number of other systems as large as itself, rolls ever silently through space in the direction of the constellation of Hercules </s>
<s> The great spheres of which it is composed spin and spin through the eternal void ceaselessly and noiselessly </s>
<s> Of these one of the smallest and most insignificant is that conglomeration of solid and of liquid particles which we have named the earth </s>
<s> It whirls onwards now as it has done before my birth, and will do after my death--a revolving mystery, coming none know whence, and going none know whither </s>
<s> Upon the outer crust of this moving mass crawl many mites, of whom I, John M'Vittie, am one, helpless, impotent, being dragged aimlessly through space </s>
<s> Yet such is the state of things amongst us that the little energy and glimmering of reason which I possess is entirely taken up with the labours which are necessary in order to procure certain metallic discs, wherewith I may purchase the chemical elements necessary to build up my ever-wasting tissues, and keep a roof over me to shelter me from the inclemency of the weather </s>
<s> I thus have no thought to expend upon the vital questions which surround me on every side </s>
<s> Yet, miserable entity as I am, I can still at times feel some degree of happiness, and am even--save the mark!--puffed up occasionally with a sense of my own importance" </s>
<s> These words, as I have said, I wrote down in my note-book, and they reflected accurately the thoughts which I found rooted far down in my soul, ever present and unaffected by the passing emotions of the hour </s>
<s> At last, however, came a time when my uncle, M'Vittie of Glencairn, died--the same who was at one time chairman of committees of the House of Commons </s>
<s> He divided his great wealth among his many nephews, and I found myself with sufficient to provide amply for my wants during the remainder of my life, and became at the same time the owner of a bleak tract of land upon the coast of Caithness, which I think the old man must have bestowed upon me in derision, for it was sandy and valueless, and he had ever a grim sense of humour </s>
<s> Up to this time I had been an attorney in a midland town in England </s>
<s> Now I saw that I could put my thoughts into effect, and, leaving all petty and sordid aims, could elevate my mind by the study of the secrets of nature </s>
<s> My departure from my English home was somewhat accelerated by the fact that I had nearly slain a man in a quarrel, for my temper was fiery, and I was apt to forget my own strength when enraged </s>
<s> There was no legal action taken in the matter, but the papers yelped at me, and folk looked askance when I met them </s>
<s> It ended by my cursing them and their vile, smoke-polluted town, and hurrying to my northern possession, where I might at last find peace and an opportunity for solitary study and contemplation </s>
<s> I borrowed from my capital before I went, and so was able to take with me a choice collection of the most modern philosophical instruments and books, together with chemicals and such other things as I might need in my retirement </s>
<s> The land which I had inherited was a narrow strip, consisting mostly of sand, and extending for rather over two miles round the coast of Mansie Bay, in Caithness </s>
<s> Upon this strip there had been a rambling, grey-stone building--when erected or wherefore none could tell me--and this I had repaired, so that it made a dwelling quite good enough for one of my simple tastes </s>
<s> One room was my laboratory, another my sitting-room, and in a third, just under the sloping roof, I slung the hammock in which I always slept </s>
<s> There were three other rooms, but I left them vacant, except one which was given over to the old crone who kept house for me </s>
<s> Save the Youngs and the M'Leods, who were fisher-folk living round at the other side of Fergus Ness, there were no other people for many miles in each direction </s>
<s> In front of the house was the great bay, behind it were two long barren hills, capped by other loftier ones beyond </s>
<s> There was a glen between the hills, and when the wind was from the land it used to sweep down this with a melancholy sough and whisper among the branches of the fir-trees beneath my attic window </s>
<s> I dislike my fellow-mortals </s>
<s> Justice compels me to add that they appear for the most part to dislike me </s>
<s> I hate their little crawling ways, their conventionalities, their deceits, their narrow rights and wrongs </s>
<s> They take offence at my brusque outspokenness, my disregard for their social laws, my impatience of all constraint </s>
<s> Among my books and my drugs in my lonely den at Mansie I could let the great drove of the human race pass onwards with their politics and inventions and tittle-tattle, and I remained behind stagnant and happy </s>
<s> Not stagnant either, for I was working in my own little groove, and making progress </s>
<s> I have reason to believe that Dalton's atomic theory is founded upon error, and I know that mercury is not an element </s>
<s> During the day I was busy with my distillations and analyses </s>
<s> Often I forgot my meals, and when old Madge summoned me to my tea I found my dinner lying untouched upon the table </s>
<s> At night I read Bacon, Descartes, Spinoza, Kant--all those who have pried into what is unknowable </s>
<s> They are all fruitless and empty, barren of result, but prodigal of polysyllables, reminding me of men who, while digging for gold, have turned up many worms, and then exhibit then exultantly as being what they sought </s>
<s> At times a restless spirit would come upon me, and I would walk thirty and forty miles without rest or breaking fast </s>
<s> On these occasions, when I used to stalk through the country villages, gaunt, unshaven, and dishevelled, the mothers would rush into the road and drag their children indoors, and the rustics would swarm out of their pot-houses to gaze at me </s>
<s> I believe that I was known far and wide as the "mad laird o' Mansie" </s>
<s> It was rarely, however, that I made these raids into the country, for I usually took my exercise upon my own beach, where I soothed my spirit with strong black tobacco, and made the ocean my friend and my confidant </s>
<s> What companion is there like the great restless, throbbing sea </s>
<s> What human mood is there which it does not match and sympathise with </s>
<s> There are none so gay but that they may feel gayer when they listen to its merry turmoil, and see the long green surges racing in, with the glint of the sunbeams in their sparkling crests </s>

<s> When it was calm in the Bay of Mansie the surface would be as clear and bright as a sheet of silver, broken only at one spot some little way from the shore, where a long black line projected out of the water looking like the jagged back of some sleeping monster </s>
<s> This was the top of the dangerous ridge of rocks known to the fishermen as the "ragged reef o' Mansie" </s>

<s> The bay itself was a bold and noble one, but too much exposed to the northern and eastern gales, and too much dreaded for its reef, to be much used by mariners </s>
<s> There was something of romance about this lonely spot </s>
<s> I have lain in my boat upon a calm day, and peering over the edge I have seen far down the flickering, ghostly forms of great fish--fish, as it seemed to me, such as naturalist never knew, and which my imagination transformed into the genii of that desolate bay </s>

<s> Clinging to the weather shrouds I could distinctly see some ten or twelve frightened seamen, who, when their light revealed my presence, turned their white faces towards me and waved their hands imploringly </s>

<s> I felt that my burden lived, for I heard the faint beat of her heart as I pressed my ear against her side in carrying her </s>

<s> from which I gathered that this piece of jetsam was both young and comely </s>
<s> * * * * * The morning after the gale was peaceful and sunny </s>
<s> As I walked along the long sweep of sand I could hear the panting of the sea </s>
<s> It was heaving and swirling about the reef, but along the shore it rippled in gently enough </s>
<s> There was no sign of the schooner, nor was there any wreckage upon the beach, which did not surprise me, as I knew there was a great undertow in those waters </s>
<s> A couple of broad-winged gulls were hovering and skimming over the scene of the shipwreck, as though many strange things were visible to them beneath the waves </s>
<s> At times I could hear their raucous voices as they spoke to one another of what they saw </s>
<s> When I came back from my walk the woman was waiting at the door for me </s>

<s> V THE GREAT BROWN-PERICORD MOTOR It was a cold, foggy, dreary evening in May </s>
<s> Along the Strand blurred patches of light marked the position of the lamps </s>
<s> The flaring shop windows flickered vaguely with steamy brightness through the thick and heavy atmosphere </s>

<s> VI THE SEALED ROOM A solicitor of an active habit and athletic tastes who is compelled by his hopes of business to remain within the four walls of his office from ten till five must take what exercise he can in the evenings </s>
<s> Hence it was that I was in the habit of indulging in very long nocturnal excursions, in which I sought the heights of Hampstead and Highgate in order to cleanse my system from the impure air of Abchurch Lane </s>

<s> One evening--it was in April or early May of the year 1894--I made my way to the extreme northern fringe of London, and was walking down one of those fine avenues of high brick villas which the huge city is for ever pushing farther and farther out into the country </s>

<s> VIII BEHIND THE TIMES My first interview with Dr </s>
<s> James Winter was under dramatic circumstances </s>
<s> It occurred at two in the morning in the bedroom of an old country house </s>
<s> I kicked him twice on the white waistcoat and knocked off his gold spectacles, while he, with the aid of a female accomplice, stifled my angry cries in a flannel petticoat and thrust me into a warm bath </s>
<s> I am told that one of my parents, who happened to be present, remarked in a whisper that there was nothing the matter with my lungs </s>
<s> I cannot recall how Dr </s>
<s> Winter looked at the time for I had other things to think of, but his description of my own appearance is far from flattering </s>
<s> A fluffy head, a body like a trussed goose, very bandy legs, and feet with the soles turned inwards--those are the main items which he can remember </s>
<s> From this time onwards the epochs of my life were the periodical assaults which Dr </s>
<s> Winter made upon me </s>
<s> He vaccinated me, he cut me for an abscess, he blistered me for mumps </s>
<s> It was a world of peace, and he the one dark cloud that threatened </s>
<s> But at last there came a time of real illness--a time when I lay for months together inside my wicker-work basket bed, and then it was that I learned that that hard face could relax, that those country-made, creaking boots could steal very gently to a bedside, and that that rough voice could thin into a whisper when it spoke to a sick child </s>
<s> And now the child is himself a medical man, and yet Dr </s>
<s> Winter is the same as ever </s>
<s> I can see no change since first I can remember him, save that perhaps the brindled hair is a trifle whiter, and the huge shoulders a little more bowed </s>
<s> He is a very tall man, though he loses a couple of inches from his stoop </s>
<s> That big back of his has curved itself over sick beds until it has set in that shape </s>
<s> His face is of a walnut brown, and tells of long winter drives over bleak country roads with the wind and the rain in his teeth </s>
<s> It looks smooth at a little distance, but as you approach him you see that it is shot with innumerable fine wrinkles, like a last year's apple </s>
<s> They are hardly to be seen when he is in repose, but when he laughs his face breaks like a starred glass, and you realise then that, though he looks old, he must be older than he looks </s>
<s> How old that is I could never discover </s>
<s> I have often tried to find out, and have struck his stream as high up as George the Fourth and even of the Regency, but without ever getting quite to the source </s>
<s> His mind must have been open to impressions very early, but it must also have closed early, for the politics of the day have little interest for him, while he is fiercely excited about questions which are entirely prehistoric </s>
<s> He shakes his head when he speaks of the first Reform Bill and expresses grave doubts as to its wisdom, and I have heard him, when he was warmed by a glass of wine, say bitter things about Robert Peel and his abandoning of the Corn Laws </s>
<s> The death of that statesman brought the history of England to a definite close, and Dr </s>
<s> Winter refers to everything which had happened since then as to an insignificant anti-climax </s>
<s> But it was only when I had myself become a medical man that I was able to appreciate how entirely he is a survival of a past generation </s>
<s> He had learned his medicine under that obsolete and forgotten system by which a youth was apprenticed to a surgeon, in the days when the study of anatomy was often approached through a violated grave </s>
<s> His views upon his own profession are even more reactionary than his politics </s>
<s> Fifty years have brought him little and deprived him of less </s>
<s> Vaccination was well within the teaching of his youth, though I think he has a secret preference for inoculation </s>
<s> Bleeding he would practise freely but for public opinion </s>
<s> Chloroform he regards as a dangerous innovation, and he always clicks with his tongue when it is mentioned </s>
<s> He has even been known to say vain things about Laennec, and to refer to the stethoscope as "a newfangled French toy" </s>
<s> He carries one in his hat out of deference to the expectations of his patients; but he is very hard of hearing, so that it makes little difference whether he uses it or not </s>
<s> He always reads, as a duty, his weekly medical paper, so that he has a general idea as to the advance of modern science </s>
<s> He persists in looking upon it, however, as a huge and rather ludicrous experiment </s>
<s> The germ theory of disease set him chuckling for a long time, and his favourite joke in the sick-room was to say, "Shut the door, or the germs will be getting in" </s>
<s> As to the Darwinian theory, it struck him as being the crowning joke of the century </s>
<s> "The children in the nursery and the ancestors in the stable," he would cry, and laugh the tears out of his eyes </s>
<s> He is so very much behind the day that occasionally, as things move round in their usual circle, he finds himself, to his own bewilderment, in the front of the fashion </s>
<s> Dietetic treatment, for example, had been much in vogue in his youth, and he has more practical knowledge of it than any one whom I have met </s>
<s> Massage, too, was familiar to him when it was new to our generation </s>
<s> He had been trained also at a time when instruments were in a rudimentary state and when men learned to trust more to their own fingers </s>
<s> He has a model surgical hand, muscular in the palm, tapering in the fingers, "with an eye at the end of each" </s>

<s> When Dr </s>
<s> Patterson and I, both of us young, energetic, and up-to-date, settled in the district, we were most cordially received by the old doctor, who would have been only too happy to be relieved of some of his patients </s>

<s> XI THE CURSE OF EVE Robert Johnson was an essentially commonplace man, with no feature to distinguish him from a million others </s>
<s> He was pale of face, ordinary in looks, neutral in opinions, thirty years of age, and a married man </s>
<s> By trade he was a gentleman's outfitter in the New North Road, and the competition of business squeezed out of him the little character that was left </s>
<s> In his hope of conciliating customers he had become cringing and pliable, until working ever in the same routine from day to day he seemed to have sunk into a soulless machine rather than a man </s>
<s> No great question had ever stirred him </s>
<s> At the end of this smug century, self-contained in his own narrow circle, it seemed impossible that any of the mighty, primitive passions of mankind could ever reach him </s>
<s> Yet birth, and lust, and illness, and death are changeless things, and when one of these harsh facts springs out upon a man at some sudden turn of the path of life, it dashes off for the moment his mask of civilisation and gives a glimpse of the stranger and stronger face below </s>
<s> Johnson's wife was a quiet little woman, with brown hair and gentle ways </s>
<s> His affection for her was the one positive trait in his character </s>
<s> Together they would lay out the shop window every Monday morning, the spotless shirts in their green cardboard boxes below, the neckties above hung in rows over the brass rails, the cheap studs glistening from the white cards at either side, while in the background were the rows of cloth caps and the bank of boxes in which the more valuable hats were screened from the sunlight </s>
<s> She kept the books and sent out the bills </s>
<s> No one but she knew the joys and sorrows which crept into his small life </s>
<s> She had shared his exultation when the gentleman who was going to India had bought ten dozen shirts and an incredible number of collars, and she had been stricken as he when, after the goods had gone, the bill was returned from the hotel address with the intimation that no such person had lodged there </s>
<s> For five years they had worked, building up the business, thrown together all the more closely because their marriage had been a childless one </s>
<s> Now, however, there were signs that a change was at hand, and that speedily </s>

<s> Doctor Miles of Bridport Place, the best man in the neighbourhood, was retained five months in advance, and, as time stole on, many little packets of absurdly small white garments with frill work and ribbons began to arrive among the big consignments of male necessities </s>

<s> It was not Robert Johnson's nature to hurry </s>

<s> Yet beneath his rough crust he was a man with a kindly heart </s>

<s> XII A MEDICAL DOCUMENT Medical men are, as a class, very much too busy to take stock of singular situations or dramatic events </s>
<s> Thus it happens that the ablest chronicler of their experiences in our literature was a lawyer </s>
<s> A life spent in watching over death-beds--or over birth-beds which are infinitely more trying--takes something from a man's sense of proportion, as constant strong waters might corrupt his palate </s>
<s> The overstimulated nerve ceases to respond </s>
<s> Ask the surgeon for his best experiences and he may reply that he has seen little that is remarkable, or break away into the technical </s>
<s> But catch him some night when the fire has spurted up and his pipe is reeking, with a few of his brother practitioners for company and an artful question or allusion to set him going </s>
<s> Then you will get some raw, green facts new plucked from the tree of life </s>
<s> It is after one of the quarterly dinners of the Midland Branch of the British Medical Association </s>
<s> Twenty coffee cups, a dozen liqueur glasses, and a solid bank of blue smoke which swirls slowly along the high, gilded ceiling gives a hint of a successful gathering </s>
<s> But the members have shredded off to their homes </s>
<s> The line of heavy, bulge-pocketed overcoats and of stethoscope-bearing top hats is gone from the hotel corridor </s>
<s> Round the fire in the sitting-room three medicos are still lingering, however, all smoking and arguing, while a fourth, who is a mere layman and young at that, sits back at the table </s>
<s> Under cover of an open journal he is writing furiously with a stylographic pen, asking a question in an innocent voice from time to time and so flickering up the conversation whenever it shows a tendency to wane </s>
<s> The three men are all of that staid middle age which begins early and lasts late in the profession </s>
<s> They are none of them famous, yet each is of good repute, and a fair type of his particular branch </s>
<s> The portly man with the authoritative manner and the white, vitriol splash upon his cheek is Charley Manson, chief of the Wormley Asylum, and author of the brilliant monograph--"Obscure Nervous Lesions in the Unmarried" </s>
<s> He always wears his collar high like that, since the half-successful attempt of a student of Revelations to cut his throat with a splinter of glass </s>
<s> The second, with the ruddy face and the merry brown eyes, is a general practitioner, a man of vast experience, who, with his three assistants and his five horses, takes twenty-five hundred a year in half-crown visits and shilling consultations out of the poorest quarter of a great city </s>
<s> That cheery face of Theodore Foster is seen at the side of a hundred sick-beds a day, and if he has one-third more names on his visiting list than in his cash-book he always promises himself that he will get level some day when a millionaire with a chronic complaint--the ideal combination--shall seek his services </s>
<s> The third, sitting on the right with his dress-shoes shining on the top of the fender, is Hargrave, the rising surgeon </s>
<s> His face has none of the broad humanity of Theodore Foster's, the eye is stern and critical, the mouth straight and severe, but there is strength and decision in every line of it, and it is nerve rather than sympathy which the patient demands when he is bad enough to come to Hargrave's door </s>
<s> He calls himself a jawman, "a mere jawman," as he modestly puts it, but in point of fact he is too young and too poor to confine himself to a specialty, and there is nothing surgical which Hargrave has not the skill and the audacity to do </s>
<s> "Before, after, and during," murmurs the general practitioner in answer to some interpolation of the outsider's </s>
<s> "I assure you, Manson, one sees all sorts of evanescent forms of madness" </s>
<s> "Ah, puerperal" </s>
<s> throws in the other, knocking the curved grey ash from his cigar </s>
<s> "But you had some case in your mind, Foster" </s>
<s> "Well, there was one only last week which was new to me </s>
<s> I had been engaged by some people of the name of Silcoe </s>
<s> When the trouble came round I went myself, for they would not hear of an assistant </s>
<s> The husband, who was a policeman, was sitting at the head of the bed on the further side </s>
<s> 'This won't do,' said I </s>
<s> 'Oh yes, doctor, it must do,' said she </s>
<s> 'It's quite irregular, and he must go,' said I </s>
<s> 'It's that or nothing,' said she </s>
<s> 'I won't open my mouth or stir a finger the whole night,' said he </s>
<s> So it ended by my allowing him to remain, and there he sat for eight hours on end </s>
<s> She was very good over the matter, but every now and again _he_ would fetch a hollow groan, and I noticed that he held his right hand just under the sheet all the time, where I had no doubt that it was clasped by her left </s>
<s> When it was all happily over, I looked at him and his face was the colour of this cigar ash, and his head had dropped on to the edge of the pillow </s>
<s> Of course I thought he had fainted with emotion, and I was just telling myself what I thought of myself for having been such a fool as to let him stay there, when suddenly I saw that the sheet over his hand was all soaked with blood; I whisked it down, and there was the fellow's wrist half cut through </s>
<s> The woman had one bracelet of a policeman's handcuff over her left wrist and the other round his right one </s>

<s> 'Aye, doctor,' said she, when she saw I had noticed it </s>
<s> 'He's got to take his share as well as me </s>
<s> Turn and turn,' said she" </s>
<s> "Don't you find it a very wearing branch of the profession" </s>
<s> asks Foster after a pause </s>
<s> "My dear fellow, it was the fear of it that drove me into lunacy work" </s>
<s> "Aye, and it has driven men into asylums who never found their way on to the medical staff </s>
<s> I was a very shy fellow myself as a student, and I know what it means" </s>
<s> "No joke that in general practice," says the alienist </s>
<s> "Well, you hear men talk about it as though it were, but I tell you it's much nearer tragedy </s>
<s> Take some poor, raw, young fellow who has just put up his plate in a strange town </s>
<s> He has found it a trial all his life, perhaps, to talk to a woman about lawn tennis and church services </s>
<s> When a young man _is_ shy he is shyer than any girl </s>
<s> Then down comes an anxious mother and consults him upon the most intimate family matters </s>

<s> Unsympathetic </s>
<s> Why, the poor lad was struck dumb and paralysed </s>

<s> "I was frightened once," says the surgeon </s>

<s> "There's no need for fiction in medicine," remarks Foster, "for the facts will always beat anything you can fancy </s>
<s> But it has seemed to me sometimes that a curious paper might be read at some of these meetings about the uses of medicine in popular fiction" </s>
<s> "How" </s>
<s> "Well, of what the folk die of, and what diseases are made most use of in novels </s>
<s> Some are worn to pieces, and others, which are equally common in real life, are never mentioned </s>
<s> Typhoid is fairly frequent, but scarlet fever is unknown </s>
<s> Heart disease is common, but then heart disease, as we know it, is usually the sequel of some foregoing disease, of which we never hear anything in the romance </s>
<s> Then there is the mysterious malady called brain fever, which always attacks the heroine after a crisis, but which is unknown under that name to the text books </s>
<s> People when they are over-excited in novels fall down in a fit </s>
<s> In a fairly large experience I have never known any one to do so in real life </s>
<s> The small complaints simply don't exist </s>
<s> Nobody ever gets shingles or quinsy, or mumps in a novel </s>
<s> All the diseases, too, belongs to the upper part of the body </s>
<s> The novelist never strikes below the belt" </s>
<s> "I'll tell you what, Foster," says the alienist, "there is a side of life which is too medical for the general public and too romantic for the professional journals, but which contains some of the richest human materials that a man could study </s>
<s> It's not a pleasant side, I am afraid, but if it is good enough for Providence to create, it is good enough for us to try and understand </s>

<s> XIV THE DOCTORS OF HOYLAND Doctor James Ripley was always looked upon as an exceedingly lucky dog by all of the profession who knew him </s>
<s> His father had preceded him in a practice in the village of Hoyland, in the north of Hampshire, and all was ready for him on the very first day that the law allowed him to put his name at the foot of a prescription </s>
<s> In a few years the old gentleman retired, and settled on the South Coast, leaving his son in undisputed possession of the whole country-side </s>
<s> Save for Doctor Horton, near Basingstoke, the young surgeon had a clear run of six miles in every direction, and took his fifteen hundred pounds a year, though, as is usual in country practices, the stable swallowed up most of what the consulting-room earned </s>
<s> Doctor James Ripley was two-and-thirty years of age, reserved, learned, unmarried, with set, rather stern features, and a thinning of the dark hair upon the top of his head, which was worth quite a hundred a year to him </s>
<s> He was particularly happy in his management of ladies </s>
<s> He had caught the tone of bland sternness and decisive suavity which dominates without offending </s>
<s> Ladies, however, were not equally happy in their management of him </s>
<s> Professionally, he was always at their service </s>
<s> Socially, he was a drop of quicksilver </s>
<s> In vain the country mammas spread out their simple lures in front of him </s>
<s> Dances and picnics were not to his taste, and he preferred during his scanty leisure to shut himself up in his study, and to bury himself in Virchow's _Archives_ and the professional journals </s>
<s> Study was a passion with him, and he would have none of the rust which often gathers round a country practitioner </s>
<s> It was his ambition to keep his knowledge as fresh and bright as at the moment when he had stepped out of the examination hall </s>
<s> He prided himself on being able at a moment's notice to rattle off the seven ramifications of some obscure artery, or to give the exact percentage of any physiological compound </s>
<s> After a long day's work he would sit up half the night performing iridectomies and extractions upon the sheep's eyes sent in by the village butcher, to the horror of his housekeeper, who had to remove the _dÃ©bris_ next morning </s>
<s> His love for his work was the one fanaticism which found a place in his dry, precise nature </s>
<s> It was the more to his credit that he should keep up to date in his knowledge, since he had no competition to force him to exertion </s>
<s> In the seven years during which he had practiced in Hoyland three rivals had pitted themselves against him, two in the village itself and one in the neighbouring hamlet of Lower Hoyland </s>
<s> Of these one had sickened and wasted, being, as it was said, himself the only patient whom he had treated during his eighteen months of ruralising </s>
<s> A second had bought a fourth share of a Basingstoke practice, and had departed honourably, while a third had vanished one September night, leaving a gutted house and an unpaid drug bill behind him </s>
<s> Since then the district had become a monopoly, and no one had dared to measure himself against the established fame of the Hoyland doctor </s>
<s> It was, then, with a feeling of some surprise and considerable curiosity that on driving through Lower Hoyland one morning he perceived that the new house at the end of the village was occupied, and that a virgin brass plate glistened upon the swinging gate which faced the high road </s>

<s> The last man had had letters half a foot long, with a lamp like a fire-station </s>
<s> Doctor James Ripley noted the difference, and deduced from it that the new-comer might possibly prove a more formidable opponent </s>

<s> No doubt Dr </s>
<s> Verrinder Smith had simply come down there in order to pursue some scientific research in peace and quiet </s>

<s> XV CRABBE'S PRACTICE I wonder how many men remember Tom Waterhouse Crabbe, student of medicine in this city </s>
<s> He was a man whom it was not easy to forget if you had once come across him </s>
